# Icon library

> The Siemens Industrial Experience design system comes with an extensive set of icons made for the industrial context. These icons are designed as in-app icons, used in the actual application UI and UI elements but not as application logos.
| ID | Name | Categories | Tags | Description | Related icons |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
